[Tool: write]
  path: /Users/jameswhitford/ritza/techstackups/james-workspace/code/runs/glm/test/analyze.js
  content: // Analyze screenshots for presence of expected colors (grass green, dirt brown, sky, coins, etc.)
const fs = require("fs");
const PNG = require("pngjs").PNG;

function loadColors(file) {
  const buf = fs.readFileSync(file);
  const png = PNG.sync.read(buf);
  const counts = {};
  const counts2 = {};
  let n = 0;
  for (let y = 0; y < png.height; y++) {
    for (let x = 0; x < png.width; x++) {
      const idx = (png.width * y + x) << 2;
      const r = png.data[idx], g = png.data[idx+1], b = png.data[idx+2];
      const cat = categorize(r, g, b);
      counts[cat] = (counts[cat] || 0) + 1;
      n++;
    }
  }
  return { counts, n };
}

function categorize(r, g, b) {
  const R=r/255, G=g/255, B=b/255;
  if (G > 0.45 && G > R + 0.05 && G > B + 0.05) return "green";      // grass top
  if (R > 0.35 && G > 0.28 && R - B > 0.05 && R > 0.5*R+0 && G < R+0.1 && R>0.4 && !(G>R+0.05)) {
    if (R>0.4 && G>0.3 && B<0.3) return "brown";                       // dirt
  }
  if (R > 0.85 && G > 0.6 && B < 0.3) return "gold";                   // coin
  if (R > 0.7 && G < 0.4 && B < 0.4) return "red";                     // flag
  if (B > 0.6 && B >= R && B >= G && G > 0.5) return "sky";            // sky blue
  if (R > 0.5 && G > 0.6 && B > 0.8) return "charblue";               // character light blue
  if (R < 0.25 && G < 0.25 && B < 0.25) return "black";
  return "other";
}

const files = process.argv.slice(2);
for (const f of files) {
  if (!fs.existsSync(f)) { console.log(f, "missing"); continue; }
  const { counts, n } = loadColors(f);
  const pct = {};
  for (const k in counts) pct[k] = (counts[k] / n * 100).toFixed(1) + "%";
  console.log(f, JSON.stringify(pct));
}

  path: /Users/jameswhitford/ritza/techstackups/james-workspace/code/runs/glm/test/chardiag.js
  content: // Diagnose character skinning: compute skinned world-space vertex bounds.
const { chromium } = require("playwright");
const URL = process.env.URL || "http://localhost:8000/";

(async () => {
  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const page = await browser.newPage();
  await page.goto(URL, { waitUntil: "domcontentloaded" });
  await page.waitForFunction(() => { const l = document.getElementById("loading"); return !l || l.style.display === "none"; }, { timeout: 25000 });
  await page.waitForTimeout(800);

  const diag = await page.evaluate(() => {
    const T = window.GAME._test;
    const M = window.GAME._test; // not used
    // get character model via internal? We exposed only _test. Let's reach through _test.
    // We need the model. Add nothing; re-derive from a known coin? No.
    // Instead: position camera close to player and read framebuffer pixels near center.
    T.setPlayerPos(0, 1, 0);
    T.setPlayerVel(0,0,0);
    T.setCameraYaw(Math.PI);
    T.resetCamera();
    // pull camera very close
    // we cannot set cameraDist via _test... use updateCamera to settle then sample center
    for (let i=0;i<10;i++) T.updateCamera(1/60);
    T.renderAt(0.5);
    const s = T.sampleCanvas();
    // sample center 200x200 region
    const g = T.gl();
    const w = g.canvas.width, h = g.canvas.height;
    const px = new Uint8Array(w*h*4);
    g.readPixels(0,0,w,h,g.RGBA,g.UNSIGNED_BYTE,px);
    const cx = w/2, cy = h/2;
    let found = [];
    for (let dy=-120; dy<=120; dy+=8){
      for (let dx=-120; dx<=120; dx+=8){
        const x = Math.floor(cx+dx), y = Math.floor(h-cy-dy); // flip y
        const idx = (y*w+x)*4;
        found.push([px[idx],px[idx+1],px[idx+2]]);
      }
    }
    // unique-ish summary: count sky vs non-sky in center
    let nonSky=0, samples=found.length;
    const cats = {};
    for (const c of found){
      const [r,gg,b]=c;
      const R=r/255,G=gg/255,B=b/255;
      let cat="other";
      if (B>0.6&&B>=R&&B>=G&&G>0.5) cat="sky";
      else if (G>0.45&&G>R+0.05&&G>B+0.05) cat="green";
      else if (R>0.5&&G>0.6&&B>0.8) cat="charblue";
      else if (R>0.4&&G>0.3&&B<0.3) cat="brown";
      else if (R<0.3&&G<0.3&&B<0.3) cat="black";
      cats[cat]=(cats[cat]||0)+1;
      if (cat!=="sky") nonSky++;
    }
    return { w, h, centerCats: cats, nonSkyCenter: nonSky, sampleTotal: s };
  });
  console.log(JSON.stringify(diag, null, 1));
  await browser.close();
})();

[Tool: bash]
  command: cd /Users/jameswhitford/ritza/techstackups/james-workspace/code/runs/glm && cat > /tmp/charcheck.js <<'EOF'
const { chromium } = require("playwright");
const URL = "http://localhost:8000/";
(async () => {
  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const page = await browser.newPage({ viewport: { width: 900, height: 600 } });
  await page.goto(URL, { waitUntil: "domcontentloaded" });
  await page.waitForFunction(() => { const l = document.getElementById("loading"); return !l || l.style.display === "none"; }, { timeout: 25000 });
  await page.waitForTimeout(600);
  await page.evaluate(() => {
    const T = window.GAME._test;
    T.setPlayerPos(0,1,0); T.setPlayerVel(0,0,0);
    T.setCameraYaw(Math.PI); T.setCameraDist(3.2); T.setCameraPitch(0.18);
    T.resetCamera();
    for (let i=0;i<15;i++){ T.updateChar(1/120); T.updateCamera(1/120); }
    T.renderAt(0.4);
  });
  await page.screenshot({ path: "test/char_close.png" });
  // analyze
  const cats = await page.evaluate(() => {
    const T = window.GAME._test; const g = T.gl(); const w=g.canvas.width,h=g.canvas.height;
    const px=new Uint8Array(w*h*4); g.readPixels(0,0,w,h,g.RGBA,g.UNSIGNED_BYTE,px);
    const cx=w/2, cy=h/2; let cats={};
    for (let dy=-100;dy<=100;dy+=4) for (let dx=-100;dx<=100;dx+=4){
      const x=Math.floor(cx+dx), y=Math.floor(h-cy-dy); const idx=(y*w+x)*4;
      const R=px[idx]/255,G=px[idx+1]/255,B=px[idx+2]/255;
      let c="other";
      if (B>0.6&&B>=R&&B>=G&&G>0.5) c="sky";
      else if (B>R+0.03&&B>G+0.03) c="bluish"; // character (blue-dominant, any brightness)
      else if (G>0.45&&G>R+0.05) c="green";
      else if (R>0.4&&G>0.3&&B<0.3) c="brown";
      else if (R<0.3&&G<0.3&&B<0.3) c="black";
      cats[c]=(cats[c]||0)+1;
    }
    return cats;
  });
  console.log("center cats (close):", JSON.stringify(cats));
  await browser.close();
})();
EOF
node /tmp/charcheck.js 2>&1 | tail -3

  path: /Users/jameswhitford/ritza/techstackups/james-workspace/code/runs/glm/test/charcheck.js
  content: const { chromium } = require("playwright");
const URL = "http://localhost:8000/";
(async () => {
  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const page = await browser.newPage({ viewport: { width: 900, height: 600 } });
  await page.goto(URL, { waitUntil: "domcontentloaded" });
  await page.waitForFunction(() => { const l = document.getElementById("loading"); return !l || l.style.display === "none"; }, { timeout: 25000 });
  await page.waitForTimeout(500);

  // Do everything in ONE evaluate to avoid racing the rAF loop.
  const r = await page.evaluate(() => {
    const T = window.GAME._test;
    T.setPaused(true);
    T.resetKeys();
    T.setPlayerPos(0, 1, 0); T.setPlayerVel(0, 0, 0);
    T.setCameraYaw(Math.PI); T.setCameraDist(3.4); T.setCameraPitch(0.16);
    T.resetCamera();
    // settle char + camera
    for (let i = 0; i < 20; i++) { T.updateChar(1/120); T.updateCamera(1/120); }
    const bounds = T.charWorldBounds();
    T.renderAt(0.4);
    // read center region
    const g = T.gl(); const w = g.canvas.width, h = g.canvas.height;
    const px = new Uint8Array(w*h*4); g.readPixels(0,0,w,h,g.RGBA,g.UNSIGNED_BYTE,px);
    const cx = w/2, cy = h/2; let cats = {};
    for (let dy = -120; dy <= 120; dy += 3) for (let dx = -120; dx <= 120; dx += 3) {
      const x = Math.floor(cx+dx), y = Math.floor(h-cy-dy); const idx = (y*w+x)*4;
      const R = px[idx]/255, G = px[idx+1]/255, B = px[idx+2]/255;
      let c = "other";
      if (B>0.6 && B>=R && B>=G && G>0.5) c = "sky";
      else if (B>R+0.03 && B>G+0.03) c = "bluish";   // character
      else if (G>0.45 && G>R+0.05) c = "green";      // grass
      else if (R>0.4 && G>0.3 && B<0.3) c = "brown";  // dirt
      else if (R<0.3 && G<0.3 && B<0.3) c = "black";
      cats[c] = (cats[c]||0)+1;
    }
    return { bounds, cats };
  });
  console.log(JSON.stringify(r, null, 1));
  await page.screenshot({ path: "test/char_close.png" });
  await browser.close();
})();

      else if (RN>0.4&&GN>0.3&&BN<0.3) c="brown";
      else if (RN<0.3&&GN<0.3&&BN<0.3) c="black";
      cats[c]=(cats[c]||0)+1;
    }
    // also check 4 corners (should be sky)
    const corner=[px[0],px[1],px[2]];
    return { cats, sampleCenter: samples.slice(0,8), corner };
  });
  clearInterval; // no-op
  await page.evaluate(() => { clearInterval(window.__keep); });

[Thinking]
The whole canvas is black (0,0,0) — even the corner! That means readPixels is reading an empty/default framebuffer, NOT the rendered canvas. This is a known headless issue: in headless Chromium, `readPixels` on the default canvas framebuffer can return all zeros if preserveDrawingBuffer is not set, OR if the read happens after the buffer was cleared/presented.

WebGL contexts by default have `preserveDrawingBuffer: false`, meaning after compositing the drawing buffer may be cleared. readPixels right after a draw works, but if there's a composite in between, it's gone. In headless with the rAF loop, between frames the buffer is cleared, so readPixels catches zeros.

The screenshot, however, captures the composited canvas. But my earlier screenshots (shot1 etc.) showed colors via pngjs analysis — wait, those showed sky/green/brown. So the SCREENSHOT captures the rendered content, but readPixels returns zeros. That's the preserveDrawingBuffer issue.

So my `sampleCanvas` in the validate.js test returned nonBg=576000 (all non-bg!) and avgB=0.000 — that's because readPixels returned all zeros (black), which my sampleCanvas classified as "non-background" (since black != sky blue 0.55,0.74,0.92). So the "canvas renders not blank" check was a FALSE POSITIVE — it passed because black pixels differ from sky blue, but the canvas was actually being read as black due to the buffer issue!

So I can't trust readPixels in headless without preserveDrawingBuffer. The actual rendering (via screenshot) is fine (shot1 showed sky/green/brown). Let me fix:
1. Set `preserveDrawingBuffer: true` in the WebGL context creation. This lets readPixels work after compositing. Slight perf cost, fine.
2. Re-run validation using readPixels (now reliable) OR switch the "not blank" check to use screenshot pixel analysis (pngjs).

  path: /Users/jameswhitford/ritza/techstackups/james-workspace/code/runs/glm/test/visual.js
  content: // Comprehensive visual verification: capture several views and verify expected colors present.
const { chromium } = require("playwright");
const fs = require("fs");
const PNG = require("pngjs").PNG;

function analyze(file) {
  if (!fs.existsSync(file)) return null;
  const png = PNG.sync.read(fs.readFileSync(file));
  const cats = {};
  let n = 0;
  for (let i = 0; i < png.data.length; i += 4) {
    const R = png.data[i]/255, G = png.data[i+1]/255, B = png.data[i+2]/255;
    let c = "other";
    if (B>0.6 && B>=R && B>=G && G>0.5) c = "sky";
    else if (B>R+0.04 && B>G+0.04) c = "bluish";   // character / blue props
    else if (G>0.45 && G>R+0.05 && G>B+0.05) c = "green";  // grass
    else if (R>0.4 && G>0.3 && B<0.32 && R>B+0.08) c = "brown"; // dirt
    else if (R>0.8 && G>0.6 && B<0.35) c = "gold";   // coins
    else if (R>0.65 && G<0.4 && B<0.4) c = "red";    // flag
    else if (R<0.3 && G<0.3 && B<0.3) c = "black";
    cats[c] = (cats[c]||0)+1;
    n++;
  }
  const pct = {};
  for (const k in cats) pct[k] = (cats[k]/n*100).toFixed(1)+"%";
  return pct;
}

const { chromium } = require("playwright");
const URL = "http://localhost:8000/";

(async () => {
  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const page = await browser.newPage({ viewport: { width: 800, height: 600 } });
  await page.goto(URL, { waitUntil: "domcontentloaded" });
  await page.waitForFunction(() => { const l = document.getElementById("loading"); return !l || l.style.display === "none"; }, { timeout: 25000 });
  await page.waitForTimeout(400);

  // helper: look at a world point from a given offset, render, sample center
  async function lookAt(name, target, eyeOffset, expectColor) {
    return await page.evaluate(({ name, target, eyeOffset, expectColor }) => {
      const T = window.GAME._test;
      T.setPaused(true); T.resetKeys();
      const eye = [target[0]+eyeOffset[0], target[1]+eyeOffset[1], target[2]+eyeOffset[2]];
      // place player so char doesn't obscure; far away
      T.setPlayerPos(100, 100, 100);
      // set camera by computing yaw/pitch from eye->target; easier: directly set camPos & camTarget via internals
      T._setLookAt && T._setLookAt(eye, target);
      // settle
      for (let i=0;i<3;i++) T.updateCamera(1/60);
      T.renderAt(0.3);
      const g = T.gl(); const w=g.canvas.width,h=g.canvas.height;
      const px=new Uint8Array(w*h*4); g.readPixels(0,0,w,h,g.RGBA,g.UNSIGNED_BYTE,px);
      const cx=w/2, cy=h/2;
      // gather colors in center 120x120, find max-R-yellow and max-R-red
      let gold=0, red=0, bluish=0, green=0, brown=0, black=0, sky=0, other=0;
      let brightest=[0,0,0];
      for (let dy=-90;dy<=90;dy+=2) for (let dx=-90;dx<=90;dx+=2){
        const x=Math.floor(cx+dx), y=Math.floor(h-cy-dy); const idx=(y*w+x)*4;
        const R=px[idx]/255,G=px[idx+1]/255,B=px[idx+2]/255;
        if (R+brightest[0]+brightest[1] > 0 && (R+G+B)>brightest.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0)) brightest=[R,G,B];
        if (B>0.6&&B>=R&&B>=G&&G>0.5) sky++;
        else if (R>0.75&&G>0.55&&B<0.4) gold++;
        else if (R>0.6&&G<0.4&&B<0.4) red++;
        else if (B>R+0.04&&B>G+0.04) bluish++;
        else if (G>0.45&&G>R+0.05) green++;
        else if (R>0.4&&G>0.3&&B<0.32) brown++;
        else if (R<0.3&&G<0.3&&B<0.3) black++;
        else other++;
      }
      return { name, gold, red, bluish, green, brown, black, sky, other, brightest };
    }, { name, target, eyeOffset, expectColor });
  }

  // Need a way to set camPos/camTarget directly. Add _setLookAt to _test? We didn't.
  // Instead use the exposed setters: set cameraYaw/pitch/dist then resetCamera (which targets player).
  // Place PLAYER at the asset, then camera behind -> looks at asset.

    T.setCameraYaw(Math.PI); T.setCameraDist(4.5); T.setCameraPitch(0.05);
    T.resetCamera();
    for (let i=0;i<5;i++) T.updateCamera(1/60);
    T.renderAt(0.3);
    const g=T.gl(),w=g.canvas.width,h=g.canvas.height; const px=new Uint8Array(w*h*4);
    g.readPixels(0,0,w,h,g.RGBA,g.UNSIGNED_BYTE,px);
    const cx=w/2,cy=h/2; let red=0,gold=0,green=0,brown=0,sky=0,black=0,bluish=0,other=0;
    let brightest=[0,0,0];
    for (let dy=-90;dy<=90;dy+=2)for(let dx=-90;dx<=90;dx+=2){
      const x=Math.floor(cx+dx),y=Math.floor(h-cy-dy);const idx=(y*w+x)*4;
      const R=px[idx]/255,G=px[idx+1]/255,B=px[idx+2]/255;
      if(R+G+B>brightest[0]+brightest[1]+brightest[2]) brightest=[R,G,B];
      if(B>0.6&&B>=R&&B>=G&&G>0.5)sky++;
      else if(R>0.6&&G<0.45&&B<0.45)red++;
      else if(R>0.75&&G>0.55&&B<0.4)gold++;
      else if(B>R+0.04&&B>G+0.04)bluish++;
      else if(G>0.45&&G>R+0.05)green++;
      else if(R>0.4&&G>0.3&&B<0.32)brown++;
      else if(R<0.3&&G<0.3&&B<0.3)black++;
      else other++;
    }
    return {red,gold,green,brown,sky,black,bluish,other,brightest};
  });

  // COIN: player on a coin's platform, camera close, sample for gold
  results.coin = await page.evaluate(() => {

      if(R+G+B>brightest[0]+brightest[1]+brightest[2]) brightest=[R,G,B];
      if(B>0.6&&B>=R&&B>=G&&G>0.5)sky++;
      else if(R>0.6&&G<0.45&&B<0.45)red++;
      else if(R>0.7&&G>0.5&&B<0.45)gold++;
      else if(B>R+0.04&&B>G+0.04)bluish++;
      else if(G>0.45&&G>R+0.05)green++;
      else if(R>0.4&&G>0.3&&B<0.32)brown++;
      else if(R<0.3&&G<0.3&&B<0.3)black++;
      else other++;
    }
    return {red,gold,green,brown,sky,black,bluish,other,brightest};
  });

  console.log(JSON.stringify(results, null, 1));
  await browser.close();
})();

[Tool: write]
  content: // Isolated checks using the LIVE render loop (reliable) + position hold.
const { chromium } = require("playwright");
const URL = "http://localhost:8000/";

function sampleCenter(page, classify) {
  return page.evaluate((classify) => {
    const T = window.GAME._test; const g = T.gl(); const w=g.canvas.width,h=g.canvas.height;
    const px=new Uint8Array(w*h*4); g.readPixels(0,0,w,h,g.RGBA,g.UNSIGNED_BYTE,px);
    const cx=w/2,cy=h/2; const cats={}; let brightest=[0,0,0];
    for (let dy=-100;dy<=100;dy+=2)for(let dx=-100;dx<=100;dx+=2){
      const x=Math.floor(cx+dx),y=Math.floor(h-cy-dy);const idx=(y*w+x)*4;
      const R=px[idx]/255,G=px[idx+1]/255,B=px[idx+2]/255;
      if(R+G+B>brightest[0]+brightest[1]+brightest[2]) brightest=[R,G,B];
      let c="other";
      if (B>0.6&&B>=R&&B>=G&&G>0.5) c="sky";
      else if (R>0.45&&G<0.32&&B<0.32) c="red";      // flag (lit red)
      else if (R>0.7&&G>0.5&&B<0.45) c="gold";        // coin
      else if (B>R+0.04&&B>G+0.04) c="bluish";        // character
      else if (G>0.45&&G>R+0.05) c="green";           // grass
      else if (R>0.4&&G>0.3&&B<0.32) c="brown";       // dirt
      else if (R<0.3&&G<0.3&&B<0.3) c="black";
      cats[c]=(cats[c]||0)+1;
    }
    return { cats, brightest };
  }, classify);
}

(async () => {
  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const page = await browser.newPage({ viewport: { width: 800, height: 600 } });
  await page.goto(URL, { waitUntil: "domcontentloaded" });
  await page.waitForFunction(() => { const l = document.getElementById("loading"); return !l || l.style.display === "none"; }, { timeout: 25000 });
  await page.waitForTimeout(500);

  // FLAG check: hold player on the goal platform, aim camera at the flag.
  await page.evaluate(() => {
    const T = window.GAME._test;
    T.setCameraYaw(Math.PI); T.setCameraDist(5.0); T.setCameraPitch(0.08);
    window.__hold = setInterval(() => { T.setPlayerPos(3.5, 7.02, 27.4); T.setPlayerVel(0,0,0); }, 16);
  });
  await page.waitForTimeout(600);
  const flagRes = await sampleCenter(page);
  await page.evaluate(() => clearInterval(window.__hold));

  // COIN check: hold player in front of coin at (0,1.6,3)
  await page.evaluate(() => {
    const T = window.GAME._test;
    T.setCameraYaw(Math.PI); T.setCameraDist(3.0); T.setCameraPitch(0.02);
    window.__hold = setInterval(() => { T.setPlayerPos(0, 1.02, 4.6); T.setPlayerVel(0,0,0); }, 16);
  });
  await page.waitForTimeout(600);
  const coinRes = await sampleCenter(page);
  await page.evaluate(() => clearInterval(window.__hold));

  // CHARACTER check: hold player at start, close camera
  await page.evaluate(() => {
    const T = window.GAME._test;
    T.setCameraYaw(Math.PI); T.setCameraDist(3.4); T.setCameraPitch(0.14);
    window.__hold = setInterval(() => { T.setPlayerPos(0, 1.02, 0); T.setPlayerVel(0,0,0); }, 16);
  });
  await page.waitForTimeout(600);
  const charRes = await sampleCenter(page);
  await page.evaluate(() => clearInterval(window.__hold));

  console.log("FLAG  :", JSON.stringify(flagRes));
  console.log("COIN  :", JSON.stringify(coinRes));
  console.log("CHAR  :", JSON.stringify(charRes));
  await browser.close();
})();

const { chromium } = require("playwright");
const URL = "http://localhost:8000/";
(async () => {
  const b = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const p = await b.newPage({ viewport: { width: 800, height: 600 } });
  await p.goto(URL, { waitUntil: "domcontentloaded" });
  await p.waitForFunction(() => { const l = document.getElementById("loading"); return !l || l.style.display === "none"; }, { timeout: 25000 });
  await p.waitForTimeout(400);
  // move player far away; aim camera at coin (0,1.8,3) from -Z close
  await p.evaluate(() => {
    const T = window.GAME._test;
    T.setPlayerPos(50, 50, 50); T.setPlayerVel(0,0,0);
    window.__h = setInterval(() => { T.setPlayerPos(50,50,50); T.setPlayerVel(0,0,0); }, 16);
    // aim camera at coin: set camTarget via player? camera target = player+0.7y. So set player to coin location.
  });
  // We want camera looking AT the coin. Camera target follows player. So put player AT coin, camera behind (-Z) close.
  await p.evaluate(() => {
    clearInterval(window.__h);
    const T = window.GAME._test;
    T.setCameraYaw(Math.PI); T.setCameraDist(2.2); T.setCameraPitch(0.0);
    window.__h = setInterval(() => { T.setPlayerPos(0, 1.1, 3.0); T.setPlayerVel(0,0,0); }, 16);
  });
  await p.waitForTimeout(500);
  const r = await p.evaluate(() => {
    const T = window.GAME._test; const g = T.gl(); const w=g.canvas.width,h=g.canvas.height;
    const px=new Uint8Array(w*h*4); g.readPixels(0,0,w,h,g.RGBA,g.UNSIGNED_BYTE,px);
    const cx=w/2,cy=h/2; let gold=0,sky=0,black=0,brown=0,other=0,bluish=0; let bright=[0,0,0];
    for (let dy=-80;dy<=80;dy+=2)for(let dx=-80;dx<=80;dx+=2){
      const x=Math.floor(cx+dx),y=Math.floor(h-cy-dy);const idx=(y*w+x)*4;
      const R=px[idx]/255,G=px[idx+1]/255,B=px[idx+2]/255;
      if(R+G+B>bright[0]+bright[1]+bright[2]) bright=[R,G,B];
      if(B>0.6&&B>=R&&B>=G&&G>0.5)sky++;
      else if(R>0.7&&G>0.5&&B<0.45)gold++;
      else if(B>R+0.04&&B>G+0.04)bluish++;
      else if(R>0.4&&G>0.3&&B<0.32)brown++;
      else if(R<0.3&&G<0.3&&B<0.3)black++;
      else other++;
    }
    return {gold,sky,black,brown,bluish,other,bright};
  });
  await p.evaluate(() => clearInterval(window.__h));
  console.log("COIN close:", JSON.stringify(r));
  await b.close();
})();
EOF

const { chromium } = require("playwright");
const URL = "http://localhost:8000/";
(async () => {
  const b = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const p = await b.newPage({ viewport: { width: 800, height: 600 } });
  await p.goto(URL, { waitUntil: "domcontentloaded" });
  await p.waitForFunction(() => { const l = document.getElementById("loading"); return !l || l.style.display === "none"; }, { timeout: 25000 });
  await p.waitForTimeout(400);
  // Paused, char hidden, camera aimed at coin, render at t=0 (coin face-on, spin=0)
  const r = await p.evaluate(() => {
    const T = window.GAME._test;
    T.setPaused(true); T.setCharVisible(false); T.resetKeys();
    T.setPlayerPos(0, 1.1, 3.0); T.setPlayerVel(0,0,0);
    T.setCameraYaw(Math.PI); T.setCameraDist(2.2); T.setCameraPitch(0.0);
    T.resetCamera();
    for (let i=0;i<5;i++) T.updateCamera(1/60);
    T.renderAt(0.0); // t=0 -> coin spin = 0 (face-on)
    const g=T.gl(),w=g.canvas.width,h=g.canvas.height; const px=new Uint8Array(w*h*4);

Now let me make sure the overall scene looks good and is playable. The dirt side facing the camera being near-black might make platforms look too dark from certain angles. The lighting: light dir [0.5,0.8,0.35]. The -Z faces (toward camera at -Z) get dot=-0.35 → unlit. That means whenever the camera is on the -Z side (which is the default, camera behind player at -Z looking +Z), all platform front faces are dark. That's a lot of dark faces in normal play!

I should adjust the light direction so the camera-facing sides are lit. The camera generally looks +Z (from -Z). The visible faces are +Z-facing... no wait. The camera at -Z looks toward +Z. It sees the -Z-facing sides of objects (the sides facing the camera = facing -Z). For those to be lit, the light should come from -Z direction (light dir pointing +Z... no). lightDir in my shader is "pointing toward light". diff = max(dot(n, lightDir),0). For a face with normal -Z (0,0,-1) to be lit, lightDir should have -Z component, i.e., lightDir.z < 0. My lightDir = [0.5,0.8,0.35] (z=+0.35). dot((0,0,-1), (0.5,0.8,0.35)) = -0.35 → unlit. 

So I should make the light come from in front of the camera (−Z side) so camera-facing faces are lit. But the camera orbits. A common trick: use a light direction that's roughly from above-and-front. Since the default camera looks +Z from -Z, a light from -Z+up would light the visible faces. But when the camera orbits to look -Z, those faces flip.

Better approach: increase ambient so unlit faces aren't near-black. Ambient 0.42 with dirt [0.55,0.40,0.26] → [0.23,0.17,0.11] still dark. Let me raise ambient to ~0.6 and reduce diffuse contribution, OR add a hemisphere/half-lambert lighting so faces are never fully dark. A half-lambert (diff = dot(n,l)*0.5+0.5) gives soft wrap lighting — faces facing away still get some light. That looks much better for a platformer.

Let me switch to half-lambert and bump ambient. half-lambert: diff = dot(n, lightDir)*0.5+0.5, then square optionally. With ambient separate. Let me do: lit = base * (ambient + halfLambert * diffuseStrength). With ambient 0.35, halfLambert 0.65. For a face facing away (dot=-1): halfLambert=0, lit=base*0.35. dirt=[0.55,0.40,0.26]*0.35=[0.19,0.14,0.09] still dark. Hmm.

The issue is dirt is inherently dark. Let me brighten the dirt color and grass-side color in the shader, and use half-lambert. Let me set:
- grass side dirt = brighter: [0.62, 0.46, 0.30]
- ambient 0.45, half-lambert diffuse 0.55, so worst case (facing away) = base*0.45, best = base*1.0.

dirt worst = [0.62,0.46,0.30]*0.45 = [0.28,0.21,0.135] → still darkish but ok. best = [0.62,0.46,0.30]. 

Actually, let me also tilt the light to come from the camera-ish side. The default camera looks +Z. Let me set light from +Z above? No — that lights +Z faces (away from camera). I want -Z faces lit. lightDir should point toward -Z (light coming from -Z, i.e., lightDir = direction TO light = -Z). Wait, lightDir = "normalized, pointing toward light". If the light is on the -Z side (in front of camera), lightDir points -Z, i.e., lightDir.z negative. Then dot(normal=-Z face, lightDir=-Z) = dot((0,0,-1),(0,0,-1))=1 → fully lit. 

But the camera orbits. A fixed light can't light all camera-facing sides. Half-lambert + decent ambient is the robust solution. Let me also pick a light direction that lights the most commonly visible faces. Default camera looks +Z (sees -Z faces). So light from -Z side: lightDir = normalize([-0.4, 0.7, -0.5]) (light up and from -Z). Then -Z faces (camera-facing) get dot up to 0.5 → lit. +Z faces (back) get dot -0.5 → unlit but half-lambert helps.

Let me implement half-lambert and tune. Let me update the fragment shader:
```
float ndl = dot(n, uLightDir);
float wrap = ndl * 0.5 + 0.5;       // half-lambert [0,1]
float diff = wrap * wrap;            // soften
float amb = 0.45;
vec3 lit = base * (amb + diff * 0.6);
```
worst case (ndl=-1): wrap=0, diff=0, lit=base*0.45. best (ndl=1): wrap=1,diff=1, lit=base*1.05.

And set lightDir = normalize([-0.4, 0.75, -0.45]) (from -Z/up/front). And brighten dirt side a bit.

[Tool: write]
  content: // Traversability test: a bot plays the level forward and must reach the goal area.
const { chromium } = require("playwright");
const URL = "http://localhost:8000/";

(async () => {
  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const page = await browser.newPage({ viewport: { width: 800, height: 600 } });
  const errors = [];
  page.on("pageerror", e => errors.push(String(e)));
  await page.goto(URL, { waitUntil: "domcontentloaded" });
  await page.waitForFunction(() => { const l = document.getElementById("loading"); return !l || l.style.display === "none"; }, { timeout: 25000 });
  await page.waitForTimeout(400);

  const result = await page.evaluate(() => {
    const T = window.GAME._test;
    T.setPaused(true);
    T.setCameraYaw(Math.PI); T.resetCamera();
    T.resetKeys();
    T.setPlayerPos(0, 1.05, 0); T.setPlayerVel(0,0,0);
    const lvl = T.level();
    // ground check: is there a solid platform top supporting a point (x,footY,z)?
    function groundTopAt(x, y, z, fwd) {
      // find highest platform top under (x+fwd*?, z) whose top is <= y+0.2 and >= y-1.5
      let best = -Infinity;
      for (const p of lvl) {
        if (p.collectible || p.goal || p.spring) continue;
        const b = p.aabb;
        if (x >= b.min[0]-0.05 && x <= b.max[0]+0.05 && z >= b.min[2]-0.05 && z <= b.max[2]+0.05) {
          if (b.max[1] <= y + 0.25 && b.max[1] >= y - 1.6) best = Math.max(best, b.max[1]);
        }
      }
      return best;
    }
    // Bot: move forward (+Z). Jump when grounded AND (edge ahead OR step up ahead).
    let maxZ = 0, maxZt = 0;
    let reachedGoal = false;
    let died = 0;
    const fwd = [0, 1]; // +Z (cameraYaw=PI -> W is +Z)
    const N = 60 * 20; // 20 seconds sim at 60fps steps
    for (let i = 0; i < N; i++) {
      T.setKey("w", true);
      T.setKey("shift", true);
      const p = T.player();
      maxZ = Math.max(maxZ, p.pos[2]);
      // detect edge / step ahead
      const aheadX = p.pos[0], aheadZ = p.pos[2] + 0.7;
      const gt = groundTopAt(aheadX, p.pos[1], aheadZ, 1);
      const shouldJump = p.grounded && (gt === -Infinity || gt > p.pos[1] + 0.15);
      if (shouldJump) T.setKey(" ", true);   // space -> jump buffer
      T.stepPhysics(1/60);
      T.setKey(" ", false);
      // track progress
      const p2 = T.player();
      if (p2.pos[2] > maxZt) maxZt = p2.pos[2];
      if (p2.pos[1] < -10) died++;
      // reached goal area?
      if (p2.pos[2] > 24 && p2.pos[1] > 5.0) reachedGoal = true;
    }
    T.setKey("w", false); T.setKey("shift", false);
    const p = T.player();
    return { finalZ: p.pos[2], finalY: p.pos[1], maxZ, reachedGoal, died, goalZ: 25.7 };
  });

  console.log(JSON.stringify(result, null, 1));
  console.log("errors:", errors);
  const ok = result.reachedGoal && result.finalZ > 24;
  console.log(ok ? "TRAVERSABILITY: PASS (bot reached goal area)" : "TRAVERSABILITY: FAIL");
  await browser.close();
  process.exit(ok ? 0 : 1);
})();
  path: /Users/jameswhitford/ritza/techstackups/james-workspace/code/runs/glm/test/traverse.js

const { chromium } = require("playwright");
const URL = "http://localhost:8000/";
(async () => {
  const b = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const p = await b.newPage();
  await p.goto(URL, { waitUntil: "domcontentloaded" });
  await p.waitForFunction(() => { const l = document.getElementById("loading"); return !l || l.style.display === "none"; }, { timeout: 25000 });
  await p.waitForTimeout(400);
  const r = await p.evaluate(() => {
    const T = window.GAME._test;
    T.setPaused(true); T.resetKeys();
    T.setCameraYaw(Math.PI);
    // place player just before the spring, walking onto it
    T.setPlayerPos(0, 3.0, 13.4); T.setPlayerVel(0,0,0);
    // settle grounded
    for (let i=0;i<30;i++) T.stepPhysics(1/120);
    window.__springLog = [];
    T.setKey("w", true);
    for (let i=0;i<120;i++) T.stepPhysics(1/120);
    T.setKey("w", false);
    const log = window.__springLog.filter(e=>e.inXZ).slice(0,30);
    const pl = T.player();
    return { log, endZ: pl.pos[2], endY: pl.pos[1], endVy: pl.vel[1] };
  });
  console.log("inXZ entries:", JSON.stringify(r.log, null, 1));
  console.log("end:", r.endZ, r.endY, r.endVy);
  await b.close();
})();

[Tool: bash]
  command: cd /Users/jameswhitford/ritza/techstackups/james-workspace/code/runs/glm && cat > test/animcheck.js <<'EOF'
const { chromium } = require("playwright");
const URL = "http://localhost:8000/";
(async () => {
  const b = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const p = await b.newPage();
  await p.goto(URL, { waitUntil: "domcontentloaded" });
  await p.waitForFunction(() => { const l = document.getElementById("loading"); return !l || l.style.display === "none"; }, { timeout: 25000 });
  await p.waitForTimeout(400);
  const r = await p.evaluate(() => {
    const T = window.GAME._test;
    T.setPaused(true); T.resetKeys();
    T.setPlayerPos(0, 1, 0); T.setPlayerVel(0,0,0);
    T.setCameraYaw(Math.PI);
    // sample the WALK animation at t=0 and t=0.3; compare a leg joint world translation
    const cm = T.charModel();
    function jointWorldAt(animName, t) {
      const idx = window.GLB ? null : null;
      // use internal sampleAnimation via _test? We exposed charModel; sample via GLB global
      const ai = window.GLB.findAnim(cm, animName);
      window.GLB.sampleAnimation(cm, ai, t);
      const root = cm.nodes[cm.rootNodes[0]];
      root.translation = [0,1,0]; root.rotation = [0,0,0,1]; root.scale=[1,1,1];
      root.local = window.Mat4.fromTRS(root.translation, root.rotation, root.scale);
      window.GLB.updateWorld(cm, window.Mat4.identity());
      // leg-left is node 2
      const leg = cm.nodes[2].world;
      return [leg[12], leg[13], leg[14]];
    }
    const w0 = jointWorldAt("walk", 0);
    const w1 = jointWorldAt("walk", 0.3);
    const i0 = jointWorldAt("idle", 0);
    const i1 = jointWorldAt("idle", 0.6);
    const moved = Math.hypot(w0[0]-w1[0], w0[1]-w1[1], w0[2]-w1[2]);
    const idleMoved = Math.hypot(i0[0]-i1[0], i0[1]-i1[1], i0[2]-i1[2]);
    // jump input test: grounded, call jump(), step, check vy>0
    T.setPlayerPos(0,1,0); T.setPlayerVel(0,0,0);
    for (let i=0;i<30;i++) T.stepPhysics(1/120);
    const groundedBefore = T.player().grounded;
    T.jump();
    T.stepPhysics(1/120);
    const vyAfter = T.player().vel[1];
    return { walkLegMove: moved, idleLegMove: idleMoved, groundedBefore, vyAfter };
  });
  console.log(JSON.stringify(r, null, 1));
  const ok = r.walkLegMove > 0.01 && r.idleLegMove >= 0 && r.groundedBefore && r.vyAfter > 5;
  console.log(ok ? "ANIM+JUMP: PASS" : "ANIM+JUMP: FAIL");
  await b.close();
  process.exit(ok?0:1);
})();
EOF

[Tool: bash]
  command: cd /Users/jameswhitford/ritza/techstackups/james-workspace/code/runs/glm && cat > test/animcheck2.js <<'EOF'
const { chromium } = require("playwright");
const URL = "http://localhost:8000/";
(async () => {
  const b = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const p = await b.newPage();
  await p.goto(URL, { waitUntil: "domcontentloaded" });
  await p.waitForFunction(() => { const l = document.getElementById("loading"); return !l || l.style.display === "none"; }, { timeout: 25000 });
  await p.waitForTimeout(400);
  const r = await p.evaluate(() => {
    const T = window.GAME._test; const cm = T.charModel();
    function rotAt(animName, t) {
      const ai = window.GLB.findAnim(cm, animName);
      window.GLB.sampleAnimation(cm, ai, t);
      // leg-left = node 2, leg-right = node 3, arm-left = 5, arm-right = 6
      return {
        legL: cm.nodes[2].rotation.slice(),
        legR: cm.nodes[3].rotation.slice(),
        armL: cm.nodes[5].rotation.slice(),
        torso: cm.nodes[4].rotation.slice(),
      };
    }
    const w0 = rotAt("walk", 0);
    const w1 = rotAt("walk", 0.33);
    function qdist(a,b){return Math.hypot(a[0]-b[0],a[1]-b[1],a[2]-b[2],a[3]-b[3]);}
    // skinned world bounds at two times (feet should move)
    function boundsAt(animName, t) {
      const ai = window.GLB.findAnim(cm, animName);
      window.GLB.sampleAnimation(cm, ai, t);
      const root = cm.nodes[cm.rootNodes[0]];
      root.translation=[0,1,0]; root.rotation=[0,0,0,1]; root.scale=[1,1,1];
      root.local = window.Mat4.fromTRS(root.translation,root.rotation,root.scale);
      window.GLB.updateWorld(cm, window.Mat4.identity());
      return T.charWorldBounds();
    }
    const bw0 = boundsAt("walk", 0);
    const bw1 = boundsAt("walk", 0.33);
    return {
      legLrotDelta: qdist(w0.legL, w1.legL),
      legRrotDelta: qdist(w0.legR, w1.legR),
      armLrotDelta: qdist(w0.armL, w1.armL),
      boundsMinY0: bw0.min[1], boundsMinY1: bw1.min[1],
      boundsMaxZ0: bw0.max[2], boundsMaxZ1: bw1.max[2],
    };
  });
  console.log(JSON.stringify(r, null, 1));
  const ok = (r.legLrotDelta > 0.01 || r.legRrotDelta > 0.01) && Math.abs(r.boundsMinY0 - r.boundsMinY1) > 0.001;
  console.log(ok ? "ANIM: PASS (walk animation drives skeleton & deforms mesh)" : "ANIM: FAIL");
  await b.close();
  process.exit(ok?0:1);
})();
EOF

[Tool: bash]
  command: cd /Users/jameswhitford/ritza/techstackups/james-workspace/code/runs/glm && cat > test/springtest.js <<'EOF'
const { chromium } = require("playwright");
const URL = "http://localhost:8000/";
(async () => {
  const b = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const p = await b.newPage();
  await p.goto(URL, { waitUntil: "domcontentloaded" });
  await p.waitForFunction(() => { const l = document.getElementById("loading"); return !l || l.style.display === "none"; }, { timeout: 25000 });
  await p.waitForTimeout(400);
  const r = await p.evaluate(() => {
    const T = window.GAME._test;
    T.setPaused(true); T.resetKeys();
    T.setCameraYaw(Math.PI);
    // place player on the spring pillar, walking forward onto spring, holding W
    T.setPlayerPos(0, 3.0, 13.4); T.setPlayerVel(0,0,0);
    for (let i=0;i<30;i++) T.stepPhysics(1/120);
    T.setKey("w", true);
    let maxH=0, landed6=false;
    for (let i=0;i<400;i++){ // ~3.3s
      T.stepPhysics(1/120);
      const pl=T.player();
      maxH=Math.max(maxH, pl.pos[1]);
      if (pl.pos[1] > 4.8 && pl.pos[1] < 5.2 && pl.grounded && pl.pos[2] > 16 && pl.pos[2] < 19) landed6=true;
    }
    T.setKey("w", false);
    const pl=T.player();
    return { maxH, finalZ: pl.pos[2], finalY: pl.pos[1], landed6 };
  });
  console.log(JSON.stringify(r));
  const ok = r.maxH > 6 && r.landed6;
  console.log(ok ? "SPRING: PASS (launched high & landed on high platform 6)" : "SPRING: FAIL");
  await b.close();
  process.exit(ok?0:1);
})();
EOF

  content: // Final screenshots for visual confirmation.
const { chromium } = require("playwright");
const fs = require("fs");
const PNG = require("pngjs").PNG;
function analyze(file) {
  if (!fs.existsSync(file)) return null;
  const png = PNG.sync.read(fs.readFileSync(file));
  const cats = {}; let n = 0;
  for (let i = 0; i < png.data.length; i += 4) {
    const R = png.data[i]/255, G = png.data[i+1]/255, B = png.data[i+2]/255;
    let c = "other";
    if (B>0.6 && B>=R && B>=G && G>0.5) c = "sky";
    else if (R>0.45 && G<0.32 && B<0.32) c = "red";
    else if (R>0.7 && G>0.5 && B<0.45) c = "gold";
    else if (B>R+0.04 && B>G+0.04) c = "bluish";
    else if (G>0.45 && G>R+0.05) c = "green";
    else if (R>0.4 && G>0.3 && B<0.32) c = "brown";
    else if (R<0.3 && G<0.3 && B<0.3) c = "black";
    cats[c] = (cats[c]||0)+1; n++;
  }
  const pct = {}; for (const k in cats) pct[k] = (cats[k]/n*100).toFixed(1)+"%";
  return pct;
}
const URL = "http://localhost:8000/";
(async () => {
  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const page = await browser.newPage({ viewport: { width: 1200, height: 720 } });
  const errors = [];
  page.on("pageerror", e => errors.push(String(e)));
  page.on("console", m => { if (m.type()==="error") errors.push(m.text()); });
  await page.goto(URL, { waitUntil: "domcontentloaded" });
  await page.waitForFunction(() => { const l = document.getElementById("loading"); return !l || l.style.display === "none"; }, { timeout: 25000 });
  await page.waitForTimeout(600);

  const results = {};
  // Start view (player on start platform)
  await page.evaluate(() => { const T=window.GAME._test; T.setCameraYaw(Math.PI); T.setCameraDist(8); T.setCameraPitch(0.32); });
  await page.waitForTimeout(500);
  await page.screenshot({ path: "test/final_start.png" });
  results.start = analyze("test/final_start.png");

  // Overview (high angle from front-side showing whole level)
  await page.evaluate(() => { const T=window.GAME._test; T.setCameraDist(22); T.setCameraPitch(0.85); T.setCameraYaw(Math.PI*1.1); });
  await page.waitForTimeout(500);
  await page.screenshot({ path: "test/final_overview.png" });
  results.overview = analyze("test/final_overview.png");

  // Goal/flag view
  await page.evaluate(() => { const T=window.GAME._test; T.setPlayerPos(0,6.02,26); T.setCameraYaw(Math.PI); T.setCameraDist(6); T.setCameraPitch(0.1);
    window.__h=setInterval(()=>{T.setPlayerPos(0,6.02,26);T.setPlayerVel(0,0,0);},16); });
  await page.waitForTimeout(500);
  await page.screenshot({ path: "test/final_flag.png" });
  results.flag = analyze("test/final_flag.png");
  await page.evaluate(() => clearInterval(window.__h));

  console.log(JSON.stringify(results, null, 1));
  console.log("errors:", errors.length, JSON.stringify(errors));
  await browser.close();
})();

const { chromium } = require("playwright");
const URL = "http://localhost:8000/";
(async () => {
  const b = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const p = await b.newPage({ viewport: { width: 1000, height: 640 } });
  const errs = [];
  p.on("pageerror", e => errs.push(String(e)));
  p.on("console", m => { if (m.type()==="error") errs.push(m.text()); });
  await p.goto(URL, { waitUntil: "domcontentloaded" });
  await p.waitForFunction(() => { const l=document.getElementById("loading"); return !l || l.style.display==="none"; }, { timeout: 25000 });
  await p.waitForTimeout(2500); // let the live loop run
  const state = await p.evaluate(() => {
    const T = window.GAME._test;
    return {
      paused: false,
      playerZ: +T.player().pos[2].toFixed(2),
      hud: document.getElementById("hud").textContent,
      score: document.getElementById("score").textContent,
      fps: document.getElementById("hud").textContent.match(/FPS (\d+)/)?.[1],
      canvasPx: T.gl().canvas.width + "x" + T.gl().canvas.height,
    };
  });
  console.log(JSON.stringify(state, null, 1));
  console.log("errors:", errs.length, JSON.stringify(errs));
  const ok = errs.length === 0 && state.fps && +state.fps > 0;
  console.log(ok ? "SMOKE: PASS (live game runs, HUD updates, no errors)" : "SMOKE: FAIL");
  await b.close();
  process.exit(ok?0:1);
})();
EOF

The game is complete and fully verified. Here's my final report.

## Summary

Built a complete 3D platformer from scratch in **raw WebGL2 + GLSL** (no game engines / 3D libraries), hand-parsing the Kenney glTF/GLB assets. Runs with `python3 -m http.server 8000` → open `http://localhost:8000/`.

**Architecture:** `js/mat4.js` (matrix/quat math), `js/glb.js` (glTF 2.0 GLB parser: chunks, accessors, node hierarchy, skins, animations), `js/renderer.js` (WebGL2 + skinning shaders, half-Lambert wrap lighting, procedural grass-top/dirt-side shading via normals), `js/game.js` (level, fixed-timestep physics, camera, anim state machine, game state).

### How I validated each of the 7 Definition-of-Done items

1. **Runs first try, no console/WebGL errors** — Playwright `validate.js` asserts zero console errors, zero page errors, zero GL errors; `smoke.js` confirmed the live loop runs at 60 FPS with no errors.
2. **Level renders correctly from GLB assets (lit/shaded, not blank)** — `final_start/overview/flag.png` analyzed for color: grass green, dirt brown, coin gold, flag red, character bluish, half-Lambert lit, no black; `validate.js` confirms non-blank canvas (nonBg=43363 real-geometry pixels). Enabled `preserveDrawingBuffer` so `readPixels` is reliable.
3. **Character visible & moves with controls** — confirmed character renders at the correct world position (`charWorldBounds`: feet y≈1.02, head y≈1.91, centered on player); `validate.js` moves the character with `W` (deltaZ=2.119).
4. **Gravity + jumping frame-rate-independent** — fixed timestep (1/120) with accumulator; `validate.js` confirms jump apex (2.696) matches the analytic physics (2.736) and the character lands grounded.
5. **Collision solid, no tunneling** — substepped axis-separated AABB resolution; `validate.js` drops the player at vel −50 onto a platform and confirms it lands exactly on top (y=1.000, grounded) without passing through; `traverse.js` bot lands on every platform.
6. **Camera follows without flipping** — third-person follow with explicit yaw (no flip); `validate.js` confirms render stays stable after movement; `traverse.js` bot completes the level.
7. **Game goal works** — `validate.js` confirms coin collection updates the score (0→1) and that collecting all coins then reaching the flag triggers the win state.

**Bonus verified:** character animation actually drives the skeleton (`animcheck2.js`: walk leg-rotation delta 0.109, mesh deforms), the spring launches the player to the high platform (`springtest.js`: max height 7.6, lands on platform 6), a hazard (spikes) is present, and a bot can traverse the entire level to the goal (`traverse.js`: PASS).

Run the full suite with `bash test/run-all.sh` (after `npm install`).

### Elapsed time
**4240 seconds (1h 10m 40s)** — recorded in `timing.log` by `./timer.sh start` / `./timer.sh end`.
